<div id="review_2359588460" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2359588460" />
    <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader"><img alt="Aj the Ravenous Reader" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557800982p2/30248594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2359588460?book_show_action=true">Apr 12, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aj the Ravenous Reader" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader">Aj the Ravenous Reader</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781484776407" href="/book/show/35099654-a-list-of-cages">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=physically-owned-books">physically-owned-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=emotionally-intense">emotionally-intense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2359588460" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16867372756355799761"><br/>An unexpected heartbreaking and yet inspiring read. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25613472.A_List_of_Cages' title='A List of Cages by Robin Roe' rel='nofollow noopener'>A List of Cages</a> is a story of an unusual friendship between an ADHD diagnosed senior superstar ( <b>Adam</b>) and a dyslexic freshman “nobody” (<b>Julian</b>). The story is told in their alternating perspectives and both their voices seem very genuine. <br/><br/>While Julian is timid and easily intimidated being a victim of domestic abuse, Adam is everybody’s darling. While nobody seems to like or care about Julian, everybody loves Adam which he doesn’t seem to notice</span>
  <span id="freeText16867372756355799761" style="display:none"><br />An unexpected heartbreaking and yet inspiring read. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25613472.A_List_of_Cages" title="A List of Cages by Robin Roe" rel="nofollow noopener">A List of Cages</a> is a story of an unusual friendship between an ADHD diagnosed senior superstar ( <b>Adam</b>) and a dyslexic freshman “nobody” (<b>Julian</b>). The story is told in their alternating perspectives and both their voices seem very genuine. <br /><br />While Julian is timid and easily intimidated being a victim of domestic abuse, Adam is everybody’s darling. While nobody seems to like or care about Julian, everybody loves Adam which he doesn’t seem to notice because he’s just genuinely kind to everybody. <br /><br />Fate must have decided to meddle with both their lives because Adam is exactly what Julian needs, someone who will see him when nobody couldn’t and through Adam, Julian finally gets to experience what it means to have friends and people (Charlie, Emerald and the rest of Adam’s gang including his mom) who care even though they’re not related to him by blood. Adam who even though is no Superman or Spiderman is definitely a hero in this story. This book is a beautiful reminder of how a small act of kindness could begin to change a person’s life. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>”Hate ricochets but kindness does too.”</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16867372756355799761" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">everyone who has a heart</span></div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4039639922454980770">A wonderful story, heartbreaking that teaches you the power of kindness and friendship just heartwarming... <b>BEAUTIFUL.</b><br/><u>Its better get into the story with knowing nothing about it but...</u><br/>Well, the two main characters are Julian a 14 year old kid that have Dyslexia and Adam a 18 year old senior who has ADHD.<br/>Julian is shy, always frightened, kind of broken, he's afraid of everything( of talking, moving, Spider-Man movies EVERYTHING) he's in freshmen year of high school but every classmate makes fun o</span>
  <span id="freeText4039639922454980770" style="display:none">A wonderful story, heartbreaking that teaches you the power of kindness and friendship just heartwarming... <b>BEAUTIFUL.</b><br /><u>Its better get into the story with knowing nothing about it but...</u><br />Well, the two main characters are Julian a 14 year old kid that have Dyslexia and Adam a 18 year old senior who has ADHD.<br />Julian is shy, always frightened, kind of broken, he's afraid of everything( of talking, moving, Spider-Man movies EVERYTHING) he's in freshmen year of high school but every classmate makes fun of him because he acts like a child and loves to read Elian Mariner's books (books that are meant for kids) maybe it is because his childhood was the best part of his life until his Parents died.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>" It's strange how many ways there are to miss someone. You miss the things they did and who they were, but you also miss who you were to them. The way everything you said and did was beautiful or entertaining or important. How much you mattered".</i>
</blockquote><br />Sad don't you think? Well gets worse <br /><br /> Adam like I said is in senior year he's popular not quite handsome or the stereotype of popular you may think he is, he is just only the most kind person in the school everyone likes him and have a very good bunch of friends everyone would've like to had they are loyal and funny.<br />All started when Adam become a counselor aide and he was assigned to "escort" Julian to his sessions with the Dr. Because he always managed to skipped it. <br /><blockquote>
  <i>""Okay, how many?"<br />He smiles and closes his eyes<br />"Ten...Thousand...Stars"".</i>
</blockquote><br />Julian's uncle Russell is a BASTARD a HUGE ASSHOLE I really really hate him, you'd know when you read it. <br /><blockquote>
  <i>" He doesn't care if you cry, but you can't fight. A sound fill the air, then pain so sharp, you feel sick, slash after slash, cutting and deep, one on top of the other. They don't stop until you're screaming into your palms" .</i>
</blockquote><br /> This book really broke my heart and restored it and broke it again. <br />Life saving, heartwarming.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>" The things I know stay in my head as I stand on my own two feet at the end of the day, and I walk back to my room with my journal to write my list of cages".</i>
</blockquote></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1806495750" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7463333498244954372">(I received an advance copy of this book for free. Thanks to Disney Book Group and NetGalley.)<br/><br/>This was a YA contemporary story, about a boy with ADHD and his younger friend.<br/><br/>Adam cared for Julian in this story, and he certainly went above and beyond to try to keep him safe and to work out what was going on with him.<br/><br/>The storyline in this was about Julian being abused, and Adam trying to help him. The pace in this was pretty slow though, and I struggled to keep reading because I was so bored. Thing</span>
  <span id="freeText7463333498244954372" style="display:none">(I received an advance copy of this book for free. Thanks to Disney Book Group and NetGalley.)<br><br>This was a YA contemporary story, about a boy with ADHD and his younger friend.<br><br>Adam cared for Julian in this story, and he certainly went above and beyond to try to keep him safe and to work out what was going on with him.<br><br>The storyline in this was about Julian being abused, and Adam trying to help him. The pace in this was pretty slow though, and I struggled to keep reading because I was so bored. Things did improve a bit towards the end, and I did feel sorry for Julian, and, yes this book was about an important subject, but I’d have appreciated it more if it had kept my interest a bit better.<br><br>The ending to this was okay, and things seemed to work out pretty well in the end.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433066531i/15045433.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>6 out of 10</span>

  <i>"People heal a whole lot faster when they're with someone who loves them."</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><i>A List of Cages</i> will be the most emotional book I read this year, I feel. It was painful. It was so damn good that I couldn't put it down. If you know me, you know I go to bed before 10pm every night without fail, I'll usually stop talking to you at 8:30pm as well. However, I was up until midnight finishing this book and crying into my pillow. <br/><br/>I've thought about this book for a week and I still can't possibly formulate</span>

If you know me, you know I go to bed before 10pm every night without fail, I'll usually stop talking to you at 8:30pm as well.   function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('PjfR1yyymEm1It+ivgLRkE75XD3I0O155ThozSJ4sVXQtmjJ++TkO9dEvwWlXPO3udRZjUqn3ATRzIixiAG5YA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('yUv8q/tVrvDbuJLwvAPMEbX8Hx6hZVvNBXSEmfUiW9EnykW1LAPSgrne8lenXe42QtEariMSarAxgGTlX1tT5A==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer5514469177064780376">Robin Roe is the author of A LIST OF CAGES, which was named one of the Best YA Books of the Year by Buzzfeed, EpicReads, BookPage, Powell’s Books, & Goodreads. <br/><br/>*Praise for A LIST OF CAGES*<br/><br/>“I love this book with my whole heart.”—Jennifer Niven, NY Times bestselling author of All the Bright Places<br/><br/>“A remarkably gripping and moving tale of a life saved—in more than one way—by the power of friendship.”</span>
  <span id="freeText5514469177064780376" style="display:none">Robin Roe is the author of A LIST OF CAGES, which was named one of the Best YA Books of the Year by Buzzfeed, EpicReads, BookPage, Powell’s Books, &amp; Goodreads. <br /><br />*Praise for A LIST OF CAGES*<br /><br />“I love this book with my whole heart.”—Jennifer Niven, NY Times bestselling author of All the Bright Places<br /><br />“A remarkably gripping and moving tale of a life saved—in more than one way—by the power of friendship.” —Emma Donoghue, best-selling author of Room.<br /><br />*“Emotion courses through every sentence of this novel, whether it is love, compassion, or bone-chilling cruelty. A triumphant story about the power of friendship and of truly being seen.”—Kirkus, starred review.<br /><br />*“A page-turner with a lot of compassion.”—Booklist, starred review.<br /><br />*“A psychologically taut tale of foster brothers unexpectedly reunited . . . Written with honesty and compassion, this book will resonate with a wide range of readers.”—Publishers Weekly, starred review.<br /><br />*“Emotional, visceral, and heartbreaking, this novel offers expertly rendered characters and beautiful language. A potent and moving work. Do not pass over this book.”—School Library Journal, starred review.<br /><br />“A LIST OF CAGES is a poignant, hopeful story about loss, grief, abuse, and the transformative power of friendship. Written with honesty and vulnerability, Robin Roe shows us exactly what it means to stand up for another person—how love and acceptance can heal even the deepest of wounds.”—Amber Smith, NY Times bestselling author of The Way I Used to Be.<br /><br />“Robin’s writing is evocative and simply beautiful; the story is raw, emotional, thought provoking and powerful. Adam and Julian have permanent homes in my heart.” —Tamara Ireland Stone, NY Times best-selling author of Every Last Word and Time Between Us.<br /><br />“A LIST OF CAGES ripped out my heart and then miraculously patched it back together. Really special. Look out for this one.”—Kelly Loy Gilbert, author of Conviction.<br /><br /><br /></span>
